        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1737032310?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Dilek VT by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/36014364-g-k-e">Gökçe</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=beautiful-love-story">beautiful-love-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=heart-warming-story">heart-warming-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=insta-lust">insta-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=adorable-characters">adorable-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=funny-hot">funny-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=hilarious">hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=light-fun-hot-romance">light-fun-hot-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1737032310" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8892782601585145823"><b>
  <i>"A sugary sweet, melting hot and heart-warming love story”</i>
</b><br/><br/>This book is like "a big chocolate cake treat", inducing euphoria... I am high above the clouds now...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472122654ra/20153879.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It put a big smile on my face and caressed my soul. I feel like a happy cat full of love...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472122654ra/20153880.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I rarely adore a heroine because they don’t usually act like I would if I were them, so they usually get on my nerves. But here, <b>she was adorable</b>. I would die for a friend like her. <br/><br/>And this book was recommended to me by my dear friend Gökçe and</span>
  <span id="freeText8892782601585145823" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"A sugary sweet, melting hot and heart-warming love story”</i>
</b><br><br>This book is like "a big chocolate cake treat", inducing euphoria... I am high above the clouds now...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472122654ra/20153879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It put a big smile on my face and caressed my soul. I feel like a happy cat full of love...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472122654ra/20153880.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I rarely adore a heroine because they don’t usually act like I would if I were them, so they usually get on my nerves. But here, <b>she was adorable</b>. I would die for a friend like her. <br><br>And this book was recommended to me by my dear friend Gökçe and I hesitated for a while knowing that the hero was a gigolo. I avoided the book for a while because I thought I would never love his story, but boy, I was so wrong. I absolutely <b>adored him</b>, too. <br><br>Don’t make my mistake and avoid reading it just because he is a gigolo. Read his story. It is sad. He doesn't want to do it. He was forced into it in some way. I believe you will love him, too.<br><br>Despite not being totally safe, I recommend this book wholeheartedly, hoping that it can also put a big smile on your face...<br><br>"A huge thank you to the writer” for this sugar-coated book, it was very sweet, indeed!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472122654ra/20153882.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, let me talk about it a little - or it will most probably be longer than a little :)))<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>Reese, our heroine, is a lovable character, beautiful inside and out. Mason, the hero, despite what he does for money, is another beautiful soul. He is beautiful inside and out, as well.<br><br>Their relationship begins as insta-lust, a sudden and huge attraction, but because of his “situation”, they cannot be more than friends for a while, but they become the best kind of friends. <br><br>Reese is more than what Mason needs, she is someone who sees "the real Mason", not the man candy only. And Mason, although he attracted her attention by his gorgeous looks first, also manages to enter her heart. <br><br>Mason is not the typical cocky gigolo. He has a “plan” – a plan to protect his family so he sacrifices himself for their good until he finishes college but Reese turns out to be the “game changer”... and what a game changer she was! Her big heart, her funny and pure spirit showed Mason that “love” can overcome all. <br><br>Reese had a bad, no the worst kind of relationship before: A psycho boyfriend who beat her, hurt her and threatened her! And when she wanted to leave him, he tried to kill her. Now, she is kilometers away from her home-town and family with a different identity.<br><br>Having lost all her trust in men, this scared beautiful girl finds her “safe haven” in Mason and they are good for each other, healing each other’s souls.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472122654i/20153884._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472122654i/20153883._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mason’s sister Sarah is also another sweet contribution to their story. I loved her existence in the novel as well.<br><br>Eva, Reese’s cousin was a bit of a puzzle for me at first, but she also ended up being OK.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br>The prologue is told by the third person. And then, the whole book is told by Reese, the heroine. And she is funny... no, she is hilarious. I couldn’t get enough of her silly and funny comments. She is now one of my favorite heroines. <br><br>And Mason -I repeat, yes, I hesitated to read this book just because he was a gigolo - but Mason being Mason made me love him. He was a great surprise indeed, not the cocky gigolo I was expecting but such a darling person. <br><br>So, if you are a romantic soul, read their beautiful and heart-warming story. <br><br>It will make you laugh.<br>It will make you sigh and swoon.<br>It will make you hot... hot hot hot.<br>It will make your heart ache.<br>It will make you cry.<br>Then, it will put all the broken pieces together and make you feel light-hearted and happy :)<br><br>At least, it did stir all these emotions in me... <br><br>*********************************************<br><br>Safety info:<br><br>Well, if you need safety in your books, then this book may upset you as there is one "blackmail sex" Mason has while being in love with Reese. He doesn't cheat on her, he just does it to protect her as he was blackmailed and it was her safety he would risk otherwise. He pukes afterwards and needs to clean himself desperately. It is a sad scene and it leaves a bitter taste... <br><br>*********************************************<br><br><i>Now, if you like, read some quotes from it and see if you like to read the rest of it...</i><br><br><b>
  <i>Okay, so maybe I was about to start drooling just the teeny tiniest bit when my cousin bumped her elbow into mine, distracting me from feasting on the hunk of man candy across the quad I might possibly have been—i.e., was totally—undressing with my gaze. <br>“Girl, don’t even think about it. You couldn’t afford him if you emptied all the money in your piggy bank.” <br>I blinked, cleared my throat, and murmured, “I’m sorry, what?” <br>“I said, uh-uh. No way. You can’t afford him.” <br>Wrinkling my nose, I kept staring because, well, really, how could I stop? He was hotness exemplified. That was my new name for him, actually: Hotness. “What? Is he, like, for sale or something?” I snickered at my own joke. <br>Eva patted my knee in a sympathetic gesture. “Yes. Actually, he is.”<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472124294i/20154340._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But seriously. He was naked under that terrycloth. Hello. Fully clothed, Mason Lowe was one hell of a yumsicle. But shirtless, he was simply indescribable.<br><br>With his hair wet, his thick locks looked extra dark—almost black—and curled even more around his ears and neck. Water droplets dripped off the clumped strands and splashed down the side of his face and throat. More beads streaked across his chest, some having the good sense to cling possessively to his über-defined guns and pecs. Not that I blamed them. If I was a droplet of water and had the great fortune of landing on Mason Lowe, I’d cleave to his muscles too.<br><br>***<br><br>I rolled my eyes and let out a big sigh. When I realized he was still just standing there, watching me, I lifted an eyebrow. “So, are you going to sit down or not?” <br>His smile fell flat. “You don’t mind?” <br><br>Mind? Sitting beside the most gorgeous guy on the planet? He obviously needed to get to know me better. The surprise in his voice made my throat go dry, however. If he could look so stunned by a girl asking him to sit by her, then it must be a rare occurrence. Did his gigolo status really make him that much of an outcast?<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472124648i/20154404._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He arched his eyebrows. “Dating? Personal life? Are you serious? The only girls who sniff around me are willing to pay or they’re looking for free services rendered, which only pisses me off.” <br>“But—” <br>“And all you monogamous, relationship-conscious ladies stay as far away from me as possible for obvious reasons.” <br>I made a face. “That can’t be true. I’m sure plenty of—” <br>“Reese.” He stopped me mid-word by lifting his hand. “Honestly, would you date a…person of my occupation?” <br>I gulped. Hells to the no, I would not. “Good point.” <br>“Yeah.” He let out a long, lonely sigh. “Exactly.” <br>“Well, that’s just sad,” I finally decided. “You can’t date or have recreational…fun, or even fall in love just because you went to drastic measures to save your family?” <br>Yes, I was feeling bad for a gigolo. Sue me.<br><br>***<br><br>“Every woman treats me that way, Reese. I’m not a person to them. I’m just…a good time or something vile to be avoided at all costs. And then you came along and you…you hugged me. You are the first person who sees me, Mason, not sex for sale.”<br><br>***<br><br>“You said we were just friends.” My voice went hoarse as I studied his taut features. “I thought—” <br><br>“We are.” He glanced away and closed his eyes. “Damn it. We are, but the only reason we’re just friends is because there’s no way we could possibly ever be anything more.”<br><br>***<br><br>“All you have to do is stretch out your hand, Mason.” Pressing my palm against my chest, I whispered, “I’m right here.” <br><br>He shook his head. “I can’t. I’m tainted.”<br><br>***<br><br>“Shh,” he murmured against my mouth just before he kissed me long and tenderly. His lips had the power to kill brain cells; it didn’t even occur to me to resist after that. <br><br>***<br><br>He nodded and kissed me, but I didn’t taste passion. This kiss was desperate and seeking; he needed reassurance that I wasn’t going to leave him. Kissing him back, I put my heart into it, and it seemed to pacify him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472122654i/20153885._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“Thank you,” he said. “I’ve always wondered what it felt like to make love.”<br><br></i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8892782601585145823" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1204287718" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1204287718" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1204287718?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=erase-this-from-my-memory">erase-this-from-my-memory</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=no-just-no">no-just-no</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1204287718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13147793189993621247">*RANT & SPOILERS AHEAD*<br/><br/>DON'T HATE ME. I know almost everyone LOVES this book and this series.<br/><br/>BUT COME ON!<br/><br/>Sweet Jesus this was like a Jerry Springer episode on crack. Between the gigolo hero, the special needs sister, the psycho ex boyfriend..it was all SO. OVER. THE. TOP. The <i>Gahs</i> and <i>Grrs</i>, and <i>Squees</i> in Reese’s thoughts. Her obsessive explanations of how hot Mason Lowe was (the first 30% of this was literally her talking about how her toes tingled every time he was near). The amount of clichés </span>
  <span id="freeText13147793189993621247" style="display:none">*RANT &amp; SPOILERS AHEAD*<br><br>DON'T HATE ME. I know almost everyone LOVES this book and this series.<br><br>BUT COME ON!<br><br>Sweet Jesus this was like a Jerry Springer episode on crack. Between the gigolo hero, the special needs sister, the psycho ex boyfriend..it was all SO. OVER. THE. TOP. The <i>Gahs</i> and <i>Grrs</i>, and <i>Squees</i> in Reese’s thoughts. Her obsessive explanations of how hot Mason Lowe was (the first 30% of this was literally her talking about how her toes tingled every time he was near). The amount of clichés (you know them: the electric jolt whenever he touched her, claiming to be falling for him after 2 conversations, the bitchy best friend, etc.) And that whole crazy ex boyfriend plot line just seemed so random.<br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/giphy_zpswipvk4of.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461277852ra/18846997.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpswipvk4of.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I thought I could handle this and overlook most of it. <br><br>I tried.<br><br>What got me the most though was how Mason decides it would be such a GREAT IDEA to to go and sleep with his landlord. Who by the way magically knows alllllllll about Reese's past, her real name, every single time her ex boyfriend hit her and in the exact location, along with her social security number, shoe size, and the last time she wiped her ass. Ok ok, so maybe she didn't know those last three things but what the fuck? Does she work for the FBI? How did she even find out about any of it? <br><br>Sorry, I digress. Back to Mason. So he sleeps with her AFTER TELLING REESE HE LOVED HER? After telling her he stopped sleeping with all those women? AFTER REESE TELLS HIM SHE LOVES HIM? I don't care about his reasoning. Just no.<br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/h_zpsk7irs7yo.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461278126ra/18847018.gif" alt=" photo h_zpsk7irs7yo.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then this (after he boinks his neighbor):<br><b>He shied away, refusing to look at me.<br>"Don't, I'm not clean."<br>..<br>"Do you want to be clean?"<br>He glanced at me, his eyes crushed yet full of hope. "Yes"<br>"Then I'll clean you."</b><br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/giphy_zpsxtkf1i0u.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461279211ra/18847092.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpsxtkf1i0u.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Hmmm, how about you stop sticking your dick in old hags, Mason? While the girl who just told you she loves you is taking care of your sister. That may help with that "clean" dilemma of yours. After Reese turned Mason sleeping with the land lady into some heroic act, I couldn't take anymore. I can't even get into all the other things that bothered me and made absolutely no sense to me, or I'd be writing this review for hours. <br><br>I know this is a ranty review, but I actually had to put my kindle down to wipe the tears from my eyes from laughing at how ridiculous and farfetched this was. <br><br>To all my book friends who loved this:<br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/4_zps1f1ridgi.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461279385ra/18847123.gif" alt=" photo 4_zps1f1ridgi.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If nothing else, this gave me a good laugh but, wow. This book was CLEARLY not for me.<br><br>Find Me On:<br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thecrazyworldofabooklover/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=100009277089211" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Page</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13147793189993621247" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_696678428" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/696678428" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/696678428?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=love">love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer696678428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9267520146743970610">4.5 Stars!!<br/><br/>Loved! This was my second book by this author and I am definitely a fan!!! This story was perfect.....it was sweet, it was funny, it was sexy, it was intriguing. I loved Reese and Mason. The writing was excellent....no cheesy dialogue.....great banter amongst the characters.....no virgin heroine.....and no insta-love. Yay!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370657ra/723497.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Reese has moved to Florida to start college after her ex boyfriend's failed murder attempt. She's taken on a new identity, is looking for a fresh start and steering </span>
  <span id="freeText9267520146743970610" style="display:none">4.5 Stars!!<br><br>Loved! This was my second book by this author and I am definitely a fan!!! This story was perfect.....it was sweet, it was funny, it was sexy, it was intriguing. I loved Reese and Mason. The writing was excellent....no cheesy dialogue.....great banter amongst the characters.....no virgin heroine.....and no insta-love. Yay!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370657ra/723497.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reese has moved to Florida to start college after her ex boyfriend's failed murder attempt. She's taken on a new identity, is looking for a fresh start and steering clear of guys and relationships. On her first day of class she spots Mason Lowe....only to be informed that he's a gigolo. Yep....that's what I said. A gigolo. <br><br>Look out Deuce!<br><br>Mason and Reese eventually become friends. Reese babysits his sister who has cerebral palsy. My heart broke for poor Mason and discovering the lengths he has gone to for his family and why and how he came to be a gigolo. Mason's clients consist of often married, rich older women--professors, neighbors, doctors included. As their friendship grows, Mason and Reese begin to have real feelings for each other. But they're both kind of stuck. Mason believes being a gigolo is the only way he can save his family and Reese knows they can never be more as long as Mason is a gigolo. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re the warm sun that shines when everything else is dark,” he went on, lifting his hands to rest them on the wall on either side of my face. “A smile and a hug in a roomful of disapproval. You’re…” Wincing, he pressed his forehead against mine. “You’re everything.”</i>
</b> <br><br>I loved the chemistry and the connection between Mason and Reese. It was HOT. I found myself begging Mason to just quit so that he and Reese could be together. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/644445.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reese is one of my favorite book heroines.....she had a great personality and she had me laughing out loud throughout the whole book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433319ra/871933.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eventually, Reese's past catches up with her. Will Mason find a way to help his family outside of being a gigolo? Can Reese ever get passed Mason's past as a gigolo? <br><br><b>
  <i>“If you love someone enough, you can make them invincible. Like your feelings for them are so strong they work as a magical shield, protecting them from all harm and pain.” </i>
</b><br><br>This story sucked me in from the very first chapter and never let go. It had great characters, the pacing of the story was perfect and it had a little bit of everything--sweet, funny, sad, smutty, drama. This was a standalone with a HEA. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9267520146743970610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer701484720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15456212660496142329"><b>☆4.5 Stars ☆ </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398862554i/9472700._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='377' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>
  <i>He could be my soul mate...expect for one tiny glitch. He is a gigolo. Boy, do I know how to pick them.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Reese is starting over, after an unfortunate turn of events, she ends up living with her cousin's family. On her first day of college she sees Mason, and is immediately interested, but there is a rumor about him.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>‘Girl don’t even think about it. You couldn’t afford him even if you emptied all the money in your piggy bank.’</b>
</i><br/><br/>So he is off limits, but they become friends and the</span>
  <span id="freeText15456212660496142329" style="display:none"><b>☆4.5 Stars ☆ </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398862554i/9472700._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="377" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>He could be my soul mate...expect for one tiny glitch. He is a gigolo. Boy, do I know how to pick them.</i>
</b><br><br>Reese is starting over, after an unfortunate turn of events, she ends up living with her cousin's family. On her first day of college she sees Mason, and is immediately interested, but there is a rumor about him.<br><br><i>
  <b>‘Girl don’t even think about it. You couldn’t afford him even if you emptied all the money in your piggy bank.’</b>
</i><br><br>So he is off limits, but they become friends and the attraction continues to grow. The sexual tension between these too was awesome. What is a girl to do, Mason is pretty damn irresistible, but Reese doesn't want to share. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398867546i/9473561._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="261" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Mason has had to make some tough choices to help support his mother and sister. At 18 he is offered an ultimatum, and becomes a gigolo. Bless his heart, I just loved his character. Mason is sweet and caring, and I hated the way he was treated. Evil ass bitches. But Reese is different, she treats him like a person, instead of something with a price tag. He wants her, but doesn't feel like he deserves her. <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398864387i/9472933._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="265" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I adored this book! I read most of this one with a huge grin on my face. Friends to lovers with forbidden love - A steamy, fun, sweet, romance with a little drama. I highly recommend!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>"You’re the warm sun that shines when everything else is dark,"</i>
</b> </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer708370261" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3102269285604220867"><b>4 1/2 "I'd Pay for That" Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435012i/878580._SX540_.jpg' width='405' height='475' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was really witty, butterfly inducing and just a good good read!<br/><br/>Reese Randall, the main character was aces in my book! She was real, sweet, funny and totally kick ass. She is in hiding from her pyscho ex and living under an alias while attending community college in Waterford with her cousin, Eva. From the first scene she is completely taken with the rumored gigolo of the town…Mason Lowe.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394570ra/759689.gif' width='405' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Mason was an extremely well written character as was his little sister</span>
  <span id="freeText3102269285604220867" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 "I'd Pay for That" Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435012i/878580._SX540_.jpg" width="405" height="475" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was really witty, butterfly inducing and just a good good read!<br><br>Reese Randall, the main character was aces in my book! She was real, sweet, funny and totally kick ass. She is in hiding from her pyscho ex and living under an alias while attending community college in Waterford with her cousin, Eva. From the first scene she is completely taken with the rumored gigolo of the town…Mason Lowe.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394570ra/759689.gif" width="405" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mason was an extremely well written character as was his little sister, Sarah. Mason has been selling himself to pay the bills for his mother and disabled sister. Mason never had a best friend or girlfriend and any intimacy he has ever encountered was paid for by his clients. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Every woman treats me that way, Reese. I’m not a person to them. I’m just…a good time or something vile to be avoided at all costs. And then you came along and you… you hugged me.”</i>
</b><br><br>What I loved most about this story was the friendship that was built off of Reese and Mason’s attraction towards one another. The progression of their relationship was perfectly paced and completely believable. I was completely giddy about this couple. <br><br><b>
  <i>"You're quirky...and yet conventional. Innocent but worldly. Reserved yet outgoing. Candid yet guarded. Trendy but also practical. And childlike while still managing to be mature. It's like...you're the perfect contradiction."</i>
</b><br><br>Reese and Mason definitely have my heart!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435012ra/878581.gif" width="405" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14034092699525143478"> <b>4 Sweet-pea scented stars! ;) </b><br/>	<br/>Meet Reese and Mason’s story. <br/>Reese is running away from her ex-boyfriend who tried to kill her and when she starts her new life in a college across the country, she meets hot and mysterious guy, Mason.<br/>Well, long story short: Mason is a gigolo. (Yeah, she sure knows how to pick them!!) <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434337i/874698.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But one night she gets a baby-sitting job and when she gets there she finds out is no one less than Mason’s little sister.   <span id="freeText14034092699525143478" style="display:none"> <b>4 Sweet-pea scented stars! ;) </b><br>	<br>Meet Reese and Mason’s story. <br>Reese is running away from her ex-boyfriend who tried to kill her and when she starts her new life in a college across the country, she meets hot and mysterious guy, Mason.<br>Well, long story short: Mason is a gigolo. (Yeah, she sure knows how to pick them!!) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434337i/874698.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But one night she gets a baby-sitting job and when she gets there she finds out is no one less than Mason’s little sister. And that’s when she finds out why he does what he does and starts to get another idea of him. After all, he’s doing it for his family, even if it means sacrifice himself. <br>So, they start as being friends. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/599597.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But soon feelings start to grow and things will eventually start to change. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434337ra/874699.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But his situation isn’t easy… or her past. <br>And how can they build something real… when she doesn’t think she can deal with is… hobby, and when he believes that he’ll never be worthy of her? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388122ra/748503.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was such and sweet and romantic book!<br>Believe, I was expecting something full of angst (and I’m kind of on a angsty-books vacation :P ) and drama… but although there was some angst and some drama it was a light and very enjoyable reading. <br>There were moments that made me want to smile and hug a pillow and the characters were pretty likeable. <br>Definitely, a book worth reading. :) </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer704306530" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1022005908401390641"><i>4 stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"…kissing you is too big of a price for me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742140i/3118002.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Reese, had the worst luck when it came to me, her first and only love turned out to be some crazed-psycho-stalker-turned-attempted-murderer, him being the main reason she is across the country hiding out at her cousin’s place. Her luck proved to be true when the man who has finally caught her eye, who made her actually feel normal, happened to be the town gigolo to the cougars. <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Resist the hunky gigolo, Reese. Resist!"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Nee</span>
  <span id="freeText1022005908401390641" style="display:none"><i>4 stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"…kissing you is too big of a price for me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742140i/3118002.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Reese, had the worst luck when it came to me, her first and only love turned out to be some crazed-psycho-stalker-turned-attempted-murderer, him being the main reason she is across the country hiding out at her cousin’s place. Her luck proved to be true when the man who has finally caught her eye, who made her actually feel normal, happened to be the town gigolo to the cougars. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Resist the hunky gigolo, Reese. Resist!"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Needing some extra cash, Reese gets a job as an evening sitter to a sweet little girl suffering from cerebral palsy, she also happens to be Mason’s little sister. It all becomes clear why he does what he does. The more time she spends in their home getting to know the little angel, has proven there is no limits to what you would do for someone you love<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He had sold his soul to ensure every bill his mother forgot to pay was taken care of, even the fricking babysitter’s bill.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Reese see’s past the gigolo, and comes to his defense time and again when he seems to just accept the gossip, she can’t believe how cruel people are, especially her cousin. Being confronted with his just proves her point that there is no future in store for them, even if she’s slowly falling for Mason. The one man who understood her, accepted her for all her quirks and ways. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Dear God. I was in love with a gigolo. It was crazy insane; I was fully aware of that. But this was Mason. My spider killer. My leftover food vacuum. My fellow Harry Potter fan. He was my soul mate. It was easy to look past the gigolo detail when I was with him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But how could it all possible work ??? She can’t expect him to stop what he is for her, there is no way he would ever stop knowing that the bills would just pile up. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I needed a freaking miracle . Or maybe a crowbar to beat some sense into him. Or maybe I needed to beat some sense into myself, because hell, I couldn’t tell which one of us was being the stupidest right now.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <i>Price of a Kiss</i>
</b> was such a sweet steamy read, I loved the parts with Reese and Mason, Reese and Sarah, Sarah and Mason, it was all so heartwarming. This had me feeling all out of whack, one moment, I’m laughing and the next I’m pissed as hell, I was so mad at their shituation. Mad at his mom, even though I know she did try, I wanted to kick the land lady’s ass for just being the ultimate cougar bitch and I especially wanted to scream at all the ignorant people they had to deal with. There was a part in the book, that I really could have done without, it broke my heart and I honestly didn’t know how to feel afterwards, like was it supposed to be okay ?!? who knows, but regardless I really enjoyed this one.</span>

  <span id="freeText2480709065188673165" style="display:none">5 IN LOVE WITH "HOTNESS" STARS!!!!<br><br>(BR with my Babes Denisse and Shannon!!)<br><br>Jen...my dear friend, why oh why didn't I read this all those months ago when you told me to?!!!!<br><br>I LOVED THIS BOOK!<br>AMAZING...simply FUCKING FANTASTIC!!<br><br>This book had me hooked from the very first page!!!<br>I'm on such a book high right now and I've met a new book boyfriend that is TOP TEN WORTHY!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps00ac4e25.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393656358i/8747060._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps00ac4e25.jpg" width="350" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Reese Randall sets her eyes on the most beautiful man she's ever seen, on her first day at Waterford County Community College.<br>"Hotness" aka Mason Lowe, is utterly drool inducing perfection.<br>She quickly hears that he's rumored to be the town gigolo.<br>Just her luck!<br>Reese doesn't have the best track record with guys.<br>Her ex, Jeremy, was physically abusive and extremely psychotic. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps17cb8264.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393656358i/8747061._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps17cb8264.jpg" width="350" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Mason Lowe, carries the weight of taking care of his little sister, Sarah, who has cerebral palsy, and helping his mom pay the rent and bills.<br>The rumors are true. <br>He is a gigolo and many of the towns wealthy cougars are his clients.<br>This is not the life he had planned for himself and if it weren't for his evil Landlady, Mrs Garrison, he probably never would have ended up in that profession.<br><br><br>The chemistry between Mason and Reese is pretty instant and WAY HOT!!<br>Circumstances keep bringing these two together and their relationship progresses slowly but this did not in any way make the story less fabulous!!<br>I loved their encounters at school and at lunch time.<br><br><br>Reese aka "Sweet Pea" was such a lovable heroine.<br>With everything that she has gone through it is a miracle that she is not a basket case.<br>She's vibrant, witty, sweet, and just about the most hilarious chick!!<br>I loved all her inner monologues, her funny banter with Mason, and her affections towards his sister, Sarah.<br><br><br>What isn't there to love about Mason?<br>He's PERFECT!<br>This guy is "HOTNESS" but he's a tortured soul.<br>He's never had sex with someone he loves. <br>Mason doesn't do "freebies".<br>He doesn't know what it is like to make love to a woman.<br><br><br>My heart broke for him.<br>The way he thought he wasn't worthy of Reese and was so desperate for her to give their relationship a chance was just tearing me up inside.<br><br><br>It takes QUITE A WHILE to get to the sexy time but HOLY HELL, when it finally happens, I swear that it is PANTY SOAKING GOOD!<br>I LITERALLY read one of the scenes a couple of times!!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_mu28gkXhFP1sk9numo1_500_zps94bb5242.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393565063ra/8732544.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mu28gkXhFP1sk9numo1_500_zps94bb5242.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I am a new fan of strawberry jam and kitchen table sex!!<br><br>I could go on forever about how AMAZING I think this book is.<br>This is a book not to be missed!<br>It's funny, sexy, and has a bit of suspense thrown in.<br>It will leave you with a big smile on your face at the end.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_m6oareKTZ81rri87i_zpscb9ae28c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393656358ra/8747062.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6oareKTZ81rri87i_zpscb9ae28c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Denisse and Shannon, you ladies are so AWESOME!<br>I loved every second of this buddy read.<br>You made it all the more of a perfect reading experience for me.<br>Love my fellow Lady Pervs!!!<br><br><br><b>From fifty yards, he'd taken my breath away. From ten feet, I'd been ready to have his babies. With a bare foot of nothing separating us in that cramped aisle between desks, there I was, on my knees in front of him.</b><br><br><br><b>But as he shifted, the terrycloth stretched down in the back, and I swear I saw a peek of crack.<br>Oh, how I could become addicted to crack, especially when those two taut, tanned globes hugging the blessed crevice molded so perfectly to the back of his towel. They were like twin mounds of ecstasy.</b><br><br><br><br><b>I wanted to keep bawling my eyes out, curl into a fetal ball, and call my mommy while drinking hot cocoa and stroking my childhood blankie.</b><br><br><br><b>Sweet baby Jesus. Talk about turning my panties to mush.</b><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I think I fell for you the moment I heard you laugh across the campus courtyard. When I looked over and saw you, I knew. You were something different. Something incredible. I knew from that first glance that nothing was ever going to be the same again. You were...a complete game changer."</b>
</i><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I love being with you, Reese."</b>
</i> <b>He looked down at my mostly naked body and let out a breath.</b> <i>
  <b>"I love doing this with you. I love...I love you, period."</b>

<span id="freeTextContainer15612236847382787661"><b>6 WONDERFUL STARS</b><br/><br/>I read this while I was on vacation and I’m JUST now getting to write my kind – of review. I remember A LOT of people recommended this book and gave it glowing reviews.<br/><br/><b>All the reviews were justified. It’s an excellent book and has everything you could want in read.</b><br/><br/>Great characters <b>Check</b><br/><br/>Great plot <b>Check</b><br/><br/>Great writing flow <b>Check</b><br/><br/>Steam <b>Check</b><br/><br/>Engaging<b>Check</b><br/><br/>Price of a Kiss was a cute and easy read. I liked how the summary doesn’t really explain anything, except for the fact the Hero is a</span>
  <span id="freeText15612236847382787661" style="display:none"><b>6 WONDERFUL STARS</b><br><br>I read this while I was on vacation and I’m JUST now getting to write my kind – of review. I remember A LOT of people recommended this book and gave it glowing reviews.<br><br><b>All the reviews were justified. It’s an excellent book and has everything you could want in read.</b><br><br>Great characters <b>Check</b><br><br>Great plot <b>Check</b><br><br>Great writing flow <b>Check</b><br><br>Steam <b>Check</b><br><br>Engaging<b>Check</b><br><br>Price of a Kiss was a cute and easy read. I liked how the summary doesn’t really explain anything, except for the fact the Hero is a gigolo. I don’t know what it is with me, but I love reading books when the Hero whore’s himself for money, it just makes a great read in my opinion.<br><br>Reese is adorable. She takes care of special needs children on the side while she goes to college. How cute is that right? I love the relationship she has with the child and it will make your heart melt.<br><br>Mason doesn’t want a relationship and doesn’t have time for that. For the time being Reese and Mason just exists in each other’s lives.<br><br>The banter and steam is off the hook. It’s just an overall happy go-lucky kind of read. You will not regret it.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17833099.Price_of_a_Kiss__Forbidden_Men___1_" title="Price of a Kiss (Forbidden Men, #1) by Linda Kage" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1375792540s/17833099.jpg" alt="Price of a Kiss (Forbidden Men, #1) by Linda Kage" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Price-Kiss-Forbidden-Men-Book-ebook/dp/B00EKLN0XO/ref=tmm_kin_swatch_0?_encoding=UTF8&amp;sr=&amp;qid=" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15612236847382787661" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1711016533248381812"><b>
  <i>***5 <u>"Hotness VS Sweet Pea"</u> stars from me***</i>
</b><br/><br/>I was very hesitate to start this book, but at the end it took me by surprise and i enjoyed it way too much!!!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443027749ra/16308237.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>So now, i can say that i'm extremely happy that i dive into this series and i'm just wondering what the next books will bring to me...<br/><i>More forbidden men??? Hell, yeah!!! But can i handle them???</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443027750i/16308238._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>You're probably wondering why this is my biggest fear... <br/><br/>Well, this story was very delightfull, but at the same time was so heartbreaking!!!<br/>I laugh</span>
  <span id="freeText1711016533248381812" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>***5 <u>"Hotness VS Sweet Pea"</u> stars from me***</i>
</b><br><br>I was very hesitate to start this book, but at the end it took me by surprise and i enjoyed it way too much!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443027749ra/16308237.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So now, i can say that i'm extremely happy that i dive into this series and i'm just wondering what the next books will bring to me...<br><i>More forbidden men??? Hell, yeah!!! But can i handle them???</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1443027750i/16308238._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>You're probably wondering why this is my biggest fear... <br><br>Well, this story was very delightfull, but at the same time was so heartbreaking!!!<br>I laugh, i smile, i had a great time, but at some point some tears blurred my vision and my heart ached so much about the heroes...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443027750ra/16308239.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Except that, i was torn badly between the right and wrong!!! My morality was in stake...<br>But i will explain you in a while what i mean by that...<br><br>Reese forced to move away from her hometown, her family, her intendity, her own life and that's because her ex violent boyfriend was obsessed with her and he tried to kill her...<br>So now, she is hiding far away from him, she was forced to throw away her dreams, she changed her name and she attended a community college...<br>The only good thing is that she had her cousin by her side to make her life seems less miserable...<br><br>One day, she spots a hottie, handsome man and she gets infatuated by him, but her cousin warns her about him...<br>There are rumors around campus that he is a gigolo...<br>That takes her by surprise but she decides to ignore that awful gossips...<br>Once or twice she comes closer to Mason and everytime she is more awe with him, but he always gets andry and mad around her... But why???<br><br>Few days later, she is attending her new job as a night babysitter for a thirteen years old girl and there are waiting for her two surprises...<br>Firstly, Sarah is having a cerebral palsy and she is in a wheel chair (That fact terrifies her!).<br>And secondly, Sarah is Mason's baby sister and he is overprotected of her...<br>But from the first moment that she is staying alone with Sarah a unique bond forced between them...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443027750ra/16308242.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And that is the key to come closer to Mason!<br><br>As the time passes and with baby steps, Mason and Reese become some kind of friends...<br>They started to know each other and that makes Reese to fell every day a little bit more in love with him...<br>They are very open with themselves... Mason admit to her that he is attending this particular job and he explain to her the reasons why he did what he did...<br>And Reese even though she knows that she can not ever be with him, she can help to inform strong feelings about him!!!<br>Even though that she gets warns all the time from her cousin and Mason himself...<br>Mason is too expensive for her pocket and he is not from these men that they will give freebies...<br>So she will decide to take whatever he wants to offer her... and this is his friendship...<br><br>And now, it's Mason's turn!!!<br>What can i say about Mason??? From the prologue already, he climb upon my heart!!!<br>I really loved that guy and he really made me to question myself many times!!!<br>Mason unwillingly got himself in a shitty situation that he couldn't escaped from it!!!<br>I felt so much pitty for him and his story!!! My soul was crying about his sake!!!<br>He was such a wonderfull guy!!! Yep, in the beginning he was distant, but as i started to know him, i fell in love with him too...<br>He was so devoted to his little family that sometimes that fact was pissing me off... Because he was sacrificing his own soul for the others...<br>He adore his little sister and he could do anything for her well-fare...<br>His messy situation broke my heart over and over again...<br>Reese was the only person that saw beyond his outside beauty and that touched something inside of him...<br>He developed strong feelings about her, but he couldn't drug her to a certain heartbroken situation. He couldn't ruin her in that way!!!<br>So he kept his distance... For good, for worse???? I can not tell you!!!<br><br>I liked Reese so much...<br>She went through so many shit with his ex, but she was still full of life...<br>Yeah, she was scared like a bitch for him to finding her for once again, but she wasn't giving up...<br>She was weird and very funny... She was so strong and non judgemental...<br>She was accepting the others the way they were...<br>Damn, she accepted Mason's job, even though she was hurting like hell inside of her...<br>She was focusing only to his outside beauty, but to his inner beauty as well... <br>She was by his side all the way...<br><br>And now, i reach the point that i will talk to you about my morality question...<br>Mason was a gigolo... He was slept with lots of women who paid him very well for that... How the hell could i adore this person???<br>And yes, i adored him... and not only me, but Reese also... <br>But i'm not in her shoes!!! That's why i admired her... She was so strong and brave...<br>I was reading the book and i was torn... I was so jealous of all the other women but at the same time i wanted like crazy for those two to be together...<br>I felt repulsive the one moment and the other i was overwelming!!! Oh, shit??? What was wrong with me???<br>And there near to the end with the landlady??? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443027750ra/16308250.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>My heart broke in small pieces and that hurt like a bitch!!! For both Mason and Reese...<br>And that's why i loved Mason very much. Because he hated himself for what he was doing but he could do anything for those who loved and i loved him just for that!!!<br><br><i>
  <b>A few more things i would like to say before i close...</b>
</i><br><b>1.</b> I really liked Linda Kage's writing and i thought that the theme was non common (at least for me!) and i found it very interesting...<br><b>2.</b> Eva annoyed the hell out of me... She was such a bitch toward Mason, but i don't have bad feelings for her and i really can not wait to found out more about her story...<br><b>3.</b> I don't want to be judgemental, but Dawn was really so ignorant???<br><b>4.</b> I loved Sarah. She was such a nice kid... I understand why all loved her so much...<br><b>5.</b> I want to tell Mason that even he thought that he didn't deserve to have Reese, my opinion is that he totally deserve her!!! Don't doubt yourself, man!!!<br><br><i>And now, i have to leave you... I have many more forbidden men to read about...</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434950868ra/15282908.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="1711016533248381812" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_677092359" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/677092359" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/677092359?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer677092359" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11354157000448830634"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430536i/863217.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My excitement about this book is still present despite the fact I finished reading it hours ago, books like this remind me exactly what I adore in New Adult novels and why I started reading them in the first place. The Price of Kiss is definitely one of the best NA books I’ve read this summer. Sexy, funny and extremely romantic story, Price of Kiss knocked my socks off and blew my mind. Linda Kage created cute and heartbreaking novel full of hilarious and passionate moments that made me laugh an</span>
  <span id="freeText11354157000448830634" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430536i/863217.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My excitement about this book is still present despite the fact I finished reading it hours ago, books like this remind me exactly what I adore in New Adult novels and why I started reading them in the first place. The Price of Kiss is definitely one of the best NA books I’ve read this summer. Sexy, funny and extremely romantic story, Price of Kiss knocked my socks off and blew my mind. Linda Kage created cute and heartbreaking novel full of hilarious and passionate moments that made me laugh and tingle in anticipation. Pure perfection!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430536i/863218.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story follow Resse Randall who flew across the country to hide from her psycho ex-boyfriend. She starts attending community college, where she meets Mason Lowe, and instantly feels attraction toward him, but mind you, it’s not book with insta love. Mason is not a boy for her, especially because he’s a gigolo. As sophisticated prostitute he’s treated poorly. Every woman sees him as a whore and nothing more. Reese knows he’s off limits but something in him pulls her toward him.<br><br>Mason is phenomenal hero, I couldn’t help but fall in love with him along with Reese. He’s a keeper, that have hard time in his life. He’s tangled in web of responsabilities that are thigting around him. My heart ached every time he spoke about being a prostitute for cougars. Reese is the only one who sees him as human and not something for sale. That’s why Mason and Reese quickly develop amazing friendship, that is the sweetest and the funniest relationship I’ve ever read about. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430536i/863219.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is awesome! I don’t know how differently describe it. It’s just hooked me and never let me go. When I finished last page I had chesire cat grin on my face and at the same time I wanted to cry it ended so soon. I wanted more! As much as I loved the ending I hoped there would be more. <br>Overall, Price of a Kiss is so good it could be stunning Hollywood movie. This is a perfect story for romance junkies, it will give you the best thrill possible! Now I know I have to read every book by Linda Kage and I’m quickly going to do so. I can’t believe someone so talented didn’t catch my attention sooner!<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11354157000448830634" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2340678485" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2340678485" />
    <a title="Penny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7463065-penny"><img alt="Penny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420145167p2/7463065.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2340678485?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Penny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Penny" href="/user/show/7463065-penny">Penny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=n-read-new-adult">n-read-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2340678485" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17987380124342221138">Actual rating 1.5 stars.<br/><br/>I can't say I enjoyed this book very much. <br/><br/>The main reason is that the story is based on many <b>sets of values and morals that I don't share</b>. And overall, is all based on generalizations. The way relationships are seen here is just not how I see life, and even though I know that most people might see things this way, I personally, don't consider it healthy. It is too limited and restricted, and as such, in my opinion, very harmful. To me, things are not good or bad, that is</span>
  <span id="freeText17987380124342221138" style="display:none">Actual rating 1.5 stars.<br /><br />I can't say I enjoyed this book very much. <br /><br />The main reason is that the story is based on many <b>sets of values and morals that I don't share</b>. And overall, is all based on generalizations. The way relationships are seen here is just not how I see life, and even though I know that most people might see things this way, I personally, don't consider it healthy. It is too limited and restricted, and as such, in my opinion, very harmful. To me, things are not good or bad, that is way too simplistic and inaccurate. <br /><br />Reese is the female protagonist, and I don't like her. Again, not because of her personality, she is a nice girl with a good heart, but because of the principals and morals she displays in her thoughts and actions. <br />Reese is very <b>judgmental</b> about Mason's profession, (which I have no problem with, his profession I mean), and although she is not as bad as her cousin, (who, by the way is in a whole other level, bigoted and classist), she is still judging, while she should be more critical instead. The way she communicates her thoughts is very irresponsible, she makes other people the reason why she doesn't do something, instead of being herself the reason, owning up to that. For example, she repeatedly says that the only reason why she is not in a relationship (romantic and sexual) with Mason, is because of Mason, because he is a gigolo. When in reality what stops her is not Mason, is herself, her set of morals. I believe that each person can have their own values, that is fine, but what I don't see right is not being aware of those being responsible for ones decisions and instead blaming others. I just can't agree with that. <br />She accepts Mason as a prostitute only if it is in the past, not in the present. She doesn't really accept him as a whole. Her love and relationship with him is CONDITIONAL of him not going back to that job, and yet she refers to her love for him in absolutist terms. It bothers me, again she is not being self aware in topics that are very fundamental to a relationship, which can end up being very harmful for everyone involved. <br />In my opinion, both Mason and Reese needed to be more critical of the situation and definitely more informed and open to other ways of conceiving life, relationships and people and their value in general. They are so limited that it prevents them from being happy, which saddens me. I find their values claustrophobic. <br /><br />What is more, I have an issue with how all the <b>women</b> that use Mason's services are portrayed. I get that there might be a few of them that could be that horrible, but here it seems like all of them are that way, and I thing is offensive, prejudiced and stereotypical. The only side contemplated here is the evil and wicked one. Again, very black and white, very unjust. <br /><br />I also have a problem with how Reese over <b>objectifies</b> Mason the moment we start reading, as well as how her attraction to him is so unrealistically described. <br /><br />Finally, I think this book is <b>politically incorrect</b> in many, many aspects. Further, the insensitive name-calling, ugh!<br /><br /><br />Now, besides all that that is based on the morals and generalizations of the book, I also have a few other reasons that prevented me from enjoying this book as mush as I would have liked:<br /><br /><b>The subplot</b> with the ex-boyfriend was very underdeveloped, predictable and cliché. It is <b>unnecessary</b> to the story and is only used as a tool to finish the book. A very lazy way to resolve a conflict that in truth in not really resolved. This is simply a patch on as a way of having a conclusion to the story in lack of something concrete. Very lackluster.<br /><br /><b>The epilogue</b> was very lame. Not far in the future at all, which for me dosen't seem enough time to round up the story and its Happy Ending, at least not in a meaningful and long-lasting way. <br /><br /><b>The whole thing </b>could have been so much richer and complex, instead is shallow and vapid. There is a huge opportunity here for critical reflection and critical thinking from the characters and we get none. <br /><br /><br />P.S.: It doesn't seem very likely that I'll ever read another romance from this author, seeing as how I will likely find the same kind of values that bother me again, and the same depthlessness.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17987380124342221138" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <b>Dear God.<br/>I was in love with a gigolo.</b>

The thing is, he is a gigolo. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492304975ra/22503991.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>As we all know, to choose this path is not easy.   <span id="freeText16079737535698480177" style="display:none"><i>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mCzLZSuOxXvexinoFE+rzF3DSBEKaOaHOO337OfE1wJ9AdJAD/21A6Zu9m8eFQNP2qvP0yqGPR1Nsegi7h5yqw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('obkpThdDmDA+myS4FmEqoW0a/pJWCUj7ZwTrSy+na8tElDBrMzDoSEYz+z8cO4Ii6nJ5UHbnk2ESWPSFJn3OYg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer5444017482651472292">Linda writes romance fiction from YA to adult, contemporary to fantasy. Most Kage stories lean more toward the lighter, funner side with a couple meaningful moments thrown in that center around love and hope. Focuses more on entertainment value and emotional impact than realism. She likes the drama and crazy, over-the-top plots that make you cry then laugh, get mad then sigh happily. <br/><br/>Published sin</span>
  <span id="freeText5444017482651472292" style="display:none">Linda writes romance fiction from YA to adult, contemporary to fantasy. Most Kage stories lean more toward the lighter, funner side with a couple meaningful moments thrown in that center around love and hope. Focuses more on entertainment value and emotional impact than realism. She likes the drama and crazy, over-the-top plots that make you cry then laugh, get mad then sigh happily. <br /><br />Published since 2010. Went through a 2-year writing correspondence class in children’s literature from The Institute of Children’s Literature. Then graduated with Bachelors in Arts, English with an emphasis in creative fiction writing from Pittsburg State University.<br /><br />Now she lives with hubby, two daughters, cat Holly, and nine cuckoo clocks in southeast Kansas, USA. Farm girl. Parents were dairy farmers. Was youngest of eight. Big family. Day job as a cataloging library assistant.<br /><br />Harry Potter House Gryffindor, Patronus White Stallion, character match Hagrid. Supernatural Team Dean. Game of Thrones Team Jon Snow and Tyrion Lannister. The Walking Dead Team Daryl. Outlander Team Jamie Fraser. Teen Wolf Team Stiles. Avenger Team Thor...or Hulk (can’t decide). Justice League Team Flash. Arrow Team Stephen Amell. Stranger Things obsessed. Heard Laurel, not Yanny.<br /><br />Started out reading with the Baby-Sitters Club. Then moved to Sandra Brown, Linda Howard, Julie Garwood, and LaVyrle Spencer in high school. Now all over the place with her romance reading tastes.<br /></span>

Or so I thought. \n\nOne night he wasn\'t quite the brainless, over-confident jerk I usually took him for.\n\nOne night, he took care of me when I was at my lowest. He opened up to me and made me open up to him.\n\nNow I\'m learning maybe he\'s not what I first thought he was. And maybe I\'M not what I first thought I was. Maybe it’s okay to rearrange a couple of my perfectly set blocks. Maybe, just maybe, I’ll stop worrying about what I’m afraid everyone else will think and finally reach for something I really want. It’s possible some of my plans need to be destroyed, and Colton Gamble is exactly the kind of mess I need in my life.\n\nWhat do you think?
